Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie; et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege, et ait .ij. petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe; et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien; puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme; et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide; et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve; et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument. Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit; et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec; et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites; puis le cure aprés .ij. jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez; et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites; puis reveigne a l’oignement.  Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	Many forms of abscess come in the womb, such as boils, inflamed abscesses, herpes, fistulas, emorroides, and other diseases that I have mentioned in the division. Therefore, it is necessary for me to say in this treatise the hot abscess that comes in the womb, which is not one of those that are covered with skin; and if you want to know about ironwork, observe whether the abscess is hard at the beginning of its arrival, and full of heat and fever, and turns red if it can be seen. Do not hasten to pierce it immediately, but let it heal until the pain subsides; then have the patient lie on one seat, and provide two small seats for him to lean against, supporting his back and spreading his legs apart; and his thighs should be spread out, and place his arms under his thighs, and tie them well with a strong rope; then bring the cow's udder towards the right side of the abdomen, and provide the tool used to open the womb, from which comes the shape; and it is necessary that when you bring this instrument, you pierce the uterus first to know its depth, so that what enters inside of the instrument does not go too deep, and does not injure the patient; and if the instrument is larger, cover the depth of the uterus with cloths, so that the instrument does not hurt it; and it must be placed on top, and marked. And when the abscess opens, and it becomes soft in the hand, it must be covered with a bandage, at the head, a linen cloth; and when the boil is empty, you must place clean lint soaked in rose oil or dry green oil in the wound; and place the lint on top of the abscess and on top of the handle with clean linen dipped in water or cooked herbs such as calendula and aristolochia. Then leave it for two days to heal with ointment, until it is healed; and sometimes the womb and the wound are lifted by enemas of water and honey, and then water or long-rooted plants such as calendula and aristolochia that have been cooked; then return to the ointment. And if the wound returns in the womb, you must guard against ironwork, but cure it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir; adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui; et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost; car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification; et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment. Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises; si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	It is necessary for the midwife to recognize the figure of natural childbirth and the signs when she sees the woman dilate downwards and desires to smell the anus: then hasten the infant to come out; thus, you understand that this childbirth occurs according to its natural form, and it is born through its head, and the afterbirth follows with it; and when you see these signs, it is necessary to press gently on the woman's abdomen so that the infant comes quickly, for when it descends towards the head, it accompanies him, and the husband rids himself of his waste by good purification. And this does not come in any other way. Sometimes it comes through its feet, or the body or chest, or hands, or abdomen, or side, and is turned accidentally on its neck, and by other evil figures; therefore, it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and skilled in these matters, and avoid error and deception, and I will show you all the figures in which one should assist.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent; et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	If the infant comes out through its head naturally and the woman gives birth painfully with weakened vitality, she should be seated on a saddle or held by women, and anoint her private parts with oil or fenugreek cooked in oil; then the midwife shall insert the small spatula-like instrument shown here:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers; et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament; puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre: si istra maintenant l’enfes.Et se les .ij. mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc; et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus .i. siege, et li lieve les piés en haut; puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement; et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	1. And cut the afterbirth (secondine), and strike its heel so that the afterbirth which is inside comes out; and seize the woman's abdomen until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then you must foment the woman with musk-root of fenugreek oil; afterwards, make her take and vomit medicine (condisi), and hold her mouth and nose for an hour: then bring forth the child.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piez	The delivery of the child over its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	If the child comes out over its feet, you must push it upwards;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	And then turn the shoulder blade gently, little by little, until it is even.
puis preigne .i. des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	Then take one piece and stretch the shoulder blade gently, little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	If it jumps up to the hips when commanded to grab, then make it vomit with a constriction.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If it jumps forward, may God will it.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it [the dislocation] is not as we have said, turn it gently until it is according to the natural figure.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	Here comes the translation: Gently turn it.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons dit, si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en .i. mortier;	And if it does not come as we have said, take musk of high quality and oil of sesame, and melted resin, and grind all in one mortar.
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement,	and put this ointment on the woman's nature inside and around it.
puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	Make him sit upright in acute agony until below the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai .i. coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when it becomes soft beneath (it), make one collyrium of myrrh, place it below, and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	Make him sit on a seat, then make him vomit and hold his mouth and nose, and press gently on the abdomen because the child is now leaping.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	From the birth of the child on its thighs
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the infant comes in this form, place its hands gently in palms.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor .i. lit;	then lay it on its neck, let its feet hang downward, and it lies on one bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	fold its hands together, then take hold of its hands above the belly and uncover the buttocks until it is exposed below.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	If the infant does not jump, take its feet and bend it forcefully, then bend it upward towards the stomach, then put your hands.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc; et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	Then make the woman hold the child with her hands until it comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	The newborn child coming out, one hand holds it from above.
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	You must devise a way to return the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	If it cannot be returned [to its place], then lift up the woman and go away.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus .i. lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she cannot walk, then lay her on a bed with her legs apart.
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	Then administer the medicine I have mentioned.
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, make her sit on a chair, then study how to return the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	Hold the child according to its natural shape, make it vomit, and command her to grasp it until the infant exits.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	For the delivery of the child on its neck, have her spread her hands and turn her face towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	The bailiff must seize his hand, then gently pull it and deliver the child.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when they are even, place the natural muscle relaxant of high altitude and oil on it, as we have said, then instruct them to move little by little.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne; et la fai esternuer.	And when you have done this, make her sit on a chair, and instruct her to take hold of it; and make her vomit.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	In the same way, administer treatment to all those affected in turn.
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes to treating them in this manner, grasp the affected area with your nail, until all moisture has been removed.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	And if the child presses on its face and neck, it causes the bone to break, which is not held, and the child dies.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	Push the child inside (into the womb), as much as you have it in the correct position, and command the woman to take herself once.
adonques si istra legierement.	Then if she gives birth easily.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the twins' birth
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent .iij. ou .iiij.; et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes triplets or quadruplets; and this is not strange, and it happens frequently.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Twins are sometimes born but they do not live, if I may name them.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know they are multiplying, and are destroyed by the scythe which divides them, which is linked to filth.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	And sometimes it happens as naturally as an animal giving birth, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if it comes out forcefully, then the treatment shall be as we have said, and let the physician be skilled, and do quickly and lightly whatever it requires.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	And do it in such a way that it is beneficial for healing.
de plusors enfans	of many children  --> multiple children (in this context)
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris .i. ou .ij. ou .iij. ou .iiij. ou .v. ou .vj. ou .vij., ou plusors jusc’a .xv., et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious,	Sometimes they are formed in the womb, one or two or three or four or five or six or seven, or more up to fifteen, and they are all formed in the shape of a child by the measurement of the holy wisdom.
et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	and it is necessary that the midwife knows this, because sometimes similar things happen.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	if it happens in this way, do as necessary.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman in labor with a dead child or abdominal pain, as I said in the division, and it does not come out forcefully, and you are forced to work by hand.
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	if you know that the woman is in good health and has no accident or fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	The woman must lie on her back, with her hips inclined downwards, and her legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de .ij. pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	The midwife should shave the woman's private parts, or tie her to the bed so she is not treated in delivering the child.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the mouth of the mother with moist oil mixed with myrrh and fennel seeds and flax seed oil, then anoint her hands with these oils and musks.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere .i. leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu,	Then insert them gently into the woman, then ask for one log of wood that will fit in the appropriate place,
et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	And take care if the infant is prepared for surgery on its head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez,	push needles into its eyes or neck or mouth or palate or under the beard or in the armpit or near the sides,
et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	and if the dislocation is on the limbs, push or hammer them back into position at their midpoints;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and it is necessary that you grip the onyx with your right hand, and place the corbeure between its two ends with your left hand, and push it gently with all your hand, and pierce the onyx into one of the places that we have mentioned, until it comes to an empty thing.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the form of the onyx:
puis fiche encontre .i. autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then pierce it against another onyx, or use three if needed, so that the extraction is equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	And then equalize it by moving from one side to the other to make it move, and hold the fingers together to keep them in place, as shown in the figure:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	If part remains, apply oil to some of his fingers and push them into that part, and pull the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	If none remains, place this finger or higher and do so until it comes out entirely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be returned due to strain.
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	Then you must fold over a cloth, until it's all covered.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	then wrap the wound at the joint or at the heel, and in this way you must do for the other hand and feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	And if the child's hips are large and narrow at birth or if it has a swollen head assembled.
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	If you must insert a splinter-like spine between your teeth, and press down on it and draw out the pus.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	you grind it with the instrument called "almidach", from which the shape comes with the tools or chapter that follows this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and in the same way, make it swell naturally if the anus becomes inflamed.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	then remove the bones with forceps.
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	And if the head of it (shoulder) jumps out and is held with force, it should be split open, as far as the moisture that is further out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	If it cannot come out, strike it into pieces at the spot where you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if it is swollen in the belly or beneath the ribs, you must pierce it until the moisture subsides.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on top of the feet, the attraction is slight, and the reduction to the mouth of the bladder is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is strangulated in the belly or the groin, you must draw it out with a cloth wrap around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and when the belly or the groin is swollen due to moisture, you should reduce the swelling;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	and if another member is set (broken), and the joint remains;
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	push the ball of your hand into the orifice of the anus, and draw it out until it reaches the mouth of the anus;
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	Then insert a small or two, and draw it through [the affected area].
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	and if the mouth of the anus is narrowed due to abscess heat that has come, it is not necessary to work on it.
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	instead, administer moist and fat substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and apply poultices, and let them rest in warm soothing and moistening liquids.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on his side, and you can make him straight, then administer what we have said in the live child.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	And if one cannot make him straight, then pull him apart piece by piece and leave nothing of the spine.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	Then when you have done this, administer what we have said in the plasters that come for marriage.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding occurs, let it be stopped with strong compression, and administer other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman whose womb had killed an infant, then consulted another about it and revived the other infants.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time an abscess came to his armpit and swelled so much that it opened and started to burst.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called for the treatment, but I thought for a long time and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I put on strong plasters with great adhesion, and an bone came out, and after several days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marvel much, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	It seemed to be the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	I sought the wound and found many bones until the woman was in better condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And the woman lived for a long time in this condition, and eventually regained a little strength.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I have not remembered this chapter except for the reason that when masters find an unusual thing, they know what to do about it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	To bring back the dislocated shoulder to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Here follows the form of the pressor, with which one weighs books; and in two turnings are the heads of the two levers.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	The horns (or probes) should be more delicate than the restriction, and made of ivory or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the rod (or probe) should be two fingers wide, and the edge of the tree (or handle) one finger, and its length half a palm;
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and within two fingers should be two equal lengths of this same rod, which are joined together at both ends, half a palm in length or slightly more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	and these two lengths are inserted into the mouth of the mallet to open when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, similar but more subtle and lighter, is to be made of ebony or boxwood, in the likeness of pincers.
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	and have two arms, two pincers, as you see, of a palm's length, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	and when you see opening the woman with all the instruments, make her sit on one bed, feet hanging down and legs apart.
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	Then put the two shoulder pieces together in the socket, and hold the head of the instrument beneath between his thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand over the entire instrument, just as you did with the tweezers equally, according to the quantity that you see opening the mouth of the socket, until the ball indicates what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	This instrument is entirely sheathed and has multiple similar parts; and when the mirror reflects them, he works more quickly and higher for humans due to their size.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not hastily prepare the instrument without first arranging it, as its necessity is not easily excused.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold in her urine, and then make her vomit with disgusting substances, and hold your hands at her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	If she jumps because of it, that is well.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If it is not so, take a pot and make a syringe or cup, and put in it herbs that can open the mouth of the woman, such as rue, anise, chamomile, caraway, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked or boiled in water over the fire; then put a cane or lid on the pot, and place the other end in the mouth of the patient.
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	and hold it until the vapors enter the patient's mouth; then make him vomit as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the second one jumps quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it remains after this treatment and does not heal as instructed, command the maidservant to wet her left hand in sesame oil or musk-scented water, then place it on it.
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and let her search for it again; and when she has found it, grasp it gently and stretch it out little by little straight, so that the man does not feel pain during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	but you must move it gently from side to side and then pull; it will come out and dislocate again.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the maw is opened wide, we have said the cure for emptying, and the fumigation of herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not all that we have said, then ensure you do not draw it out.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that the one at the mouth of the maw, you tie it to the thigh of the woman, then you cleanse it with ointment trifarmaçon.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	if it will persist and return, and become feverish; but nevertheless, when it comes and causes bad smell in the stomach and head, it will hurt the sick person.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	Therefore, it is necessary to use suitable fumigations for this purpose: no one of the ancients has proven fumigation with dill and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument used for fumigating a woman to retain flowers and afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is shaped like glass resembling a cane, and the narrow part is inserted into the body, and the wide parts are placed over the fire.
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And let the fumigation be over the coals, and the tinea until it is destroyed, and begin another.
de percier lou fondement	To drill the foundation.
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foundation drilled, but it has been stopped up with a subtle syrup:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, instruct the maidservant to pierce him with a lance at his due place, and not pierce him with a sharp spur, and guard the opening so that it is not touched.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Next put wool soaked in wine and oil on it, then treat with an ointment until it heals.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it does not recur, put or place a plum stone there, and leave it for many days, and it should be removed when the patient is seen to go to bed.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes this plugging of wounds or abscesses occurs; it is necessary to cover the wound in this way: if it heals, as we have said with a plum stone.
de la fistule dou fondement	From the fistula base
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from the base are nodules, and larger than those that come out of the side of the foundation, or in the space between two parts,
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	if there is one or more fistulas; and when the nodulation is old, it becomes inflamed, and moisture wakes up pus or thin boils,
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And sometimes they are Persian fistula; and they are recognized by this, that there is either evacuation or windiness when the patient evacuates, and possibly it may jump out one side.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if they penetrate up to the bladder, and up to half of the penis; and they reach the junction of the thigh, and up to the nut of the calf.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes the Persian fistula by its foundation, and not the non-Persian fistula:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And you shall bite your tooth index or foundation, and insert a fine awl of bronze or iron into the fistula when there is no twist.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	If there is a twist, insert a thin splint or horse hair until you feel the splint or the hair at your tooth.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	If you do not understand it and no blood, pus, wind, or urine comes out as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	Know that it does not pierce at all; hasten to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula penetrates up to the bladder or leads to the conduit of urine, if it shoots out urine and cannot be sealed with medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced up to the junction of the calf, then the tendon comes out to its place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if it is not twisted and there is no injury around the pain, then it remains thus, and no medicine or binding with ointment is of use.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in these Persian bladders, there is no remedy but work, and the foolish doctors' vain attempts who involve themselves with it.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In that which is not Persian nor old, in hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced.
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and it is that the sick person lies between your hands on his back; and have the legs lifted up to the thighs, and have the thighs inclined towards the belly.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then push a tent of iron, or wood if there is a curvature, as long as you know where the dislocation comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the patient feels it around the foundation, then you must place your finger there.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	If it is felt that the dislocation has penetrated through; and if it is uncovered where you feel between your finger or flesh, then you know that it is pierced.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If one does not work on it, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	However, one can heal some, but it happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And the help that one gives, it is heating the cautery subtle according to the width of the wound, as it has been said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	And push everything hot into the fistula until it comes out from the base; and do this 2 or 3 times, as you know that these charred pieces should be burned, which resemble a bird's quill.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	Then cure the burn with damp cloths soaked in butter until the char is gone, then cure it with a healing ointment made of burning char and resin.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it heals in this way, that is good. But if it cannot heal otherwise;   And to make sure that the wound does not become infected, apply some medicinal herbs and keep it covered with a dressing:   Et pour ce que le maulx ne soient a la grant plaie, mette de bonnes herbes medicinales et couvres le d’un emplastre.
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if it tries to enter [the wound], and does not pierce as far as the base which is the foundation, and between your finger and the tent you place a thick covering of flesh or of syfac, and you see the fistula at the place where the covering is cut;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the tip of the fistula approaches and presses against the tent, and then the cautery is applied after that, until it reaches the top of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	And the tent is released and it will tear; then take out those fatty tissues that seem like a feather of a bird, and nothing remains.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the bone breaks through [the skin], and pierces you, either burn it with fire or apply a medicinal cure.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	The fire cautery consists of two things: namely, the burning of these adjacent charred areas, and the stopping of blood flow and the drying of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then apply the treatment for wet tents in butter or cooked cheese until the wound fills with pus and the charred areas are covered in it.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with onions soaked in hard charcoal and dry medications.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	When it is reset, it heals and does not dislocate again.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	If a fistula comes up to the surface of the foundation and is separated from the body, push your thumb or the foundation into it and probe it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel a tumor, and there are two layers or the membrane or charms, where it is almost ready to pierce, but has no other way of healing or hope except by one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you burn it as we have said, or you strike it to the bottom, or if possible you put pressure on it and treat it as first aid;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, so you do not cover the holding element that supports the base, and let the evacuations come through voluntary sensation;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then heal it, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	By chance it will be healthy, or you remove that covering and clean it after it is cut off at the base, either by force or by another tool specified.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then fill in the cavity in the wound as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	Then study to restore the wound and keep the fistula in the area beyond the base: it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes there are fistulas of this kind: and it is when you press the edge of the fistula against the base of the skin above,   \]
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	If one takes a tent peg pierced through the head according to this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And put .i. thread twisted in .ij., and push the tent peg through the entire length of the thread into the fistula until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is pierced in the margin of the foundation within, then pull out that thread, so that you push your finger or base to:
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	And draw out the head with thread, and join the two shoulders together, and hold one to the other, and leave it for one day or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And do not tighten it at any time until the threads seize those things that are between them and they stick together;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then heal the wound until it is healed and healthy.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open by itself, make it open in all possible ways as you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	It is not advisable to cover a wound with a plaster while it is healing, as previously mentioned, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the pointed spinal splint used to make a fistula is very sharp at both ends and cuts.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other hand, it is not covered because one should not cover what one should not cover, as you see here:  (This suggests that covering a wound with a plaster should only be done when necessary)
des emorroydes	hemorrhoids   (medical condition characterized by the swelling of veins in the rectum and anus)
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Emorydes (emolients) are of two kinds: they are within the foundation, like a grain of resin, and there are small and large ones, and on the outside there is blood.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	and there is one or more, and they are outside the foundation and away from the base of the foundation; but those that are away have little moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	and they have a yellowish tinge or a small amount of blood and are the color of the body.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the cure for those that have them within the foundation is to instruct the patient to cough, so that the foundation loosens and the phlegm appears.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you hurry, you hold it with tongs or take hold of it with your nail, then strike at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if they cannot hold it with their moisture, you take hold of it with cloth or gauze, or a piece of linen;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and you pull them towards your fingers, then strike, and sprinkle some hot powders on top as a substitute for the cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize them as said in the chapter of cautery, then you cure them with other treatments until they are healthy.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundation cannot come out, you clisterize the patient with biting and harsh clisteria to clean where the foundation is, so that it can come out openly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	if the patients prepare themselves and the threads are far from the foundation, then the cure is easy;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And it is that you grab them with your nail or tweezers, strike them, then heal them as we have said, until they are healthy and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	It is necessary that you make the stitch in this way: take one twisted thread and insert it into a needle, then draw the thread above and pierce the needle from the other side, and twist the two ends of the thread below the needle.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is wide; draw the thread tightly, then knot the thread, remove the needle, and do the same for all the others, leaving one hole for drainage of excess blood.
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place a soft cloth moistened in rose oil or turpentine on the foundation, and place it there, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then leave it until it stops dripping, and when it is dry, treat it with ointment and other treatments until it heals.

Often there is a drying of fevers in the intestines and due to natural constraint; and when the disease is old and medication has no effect.
